    "# === Build \"All Equations & Figures\" PDF for Hodge + HodgeClean (no inline color tags) ===\n",
    "from pathlib import Path\n",
    "from datetime import datetime, timezone\n",
    "import re\n",
    "import matplotlib\n",
    "matplotlib.use(\"Agg\")\n",
    "import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n",
    "from reportlab.platypus import SimpleDocTemplate, Paragraph, Spacer, PageBreak, Image, KeepTogether\n",
    "from reportlab.lib.styles import getSampleStyleSheet, ParagraphStyle\n",
    "from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter\n",
    "from reportlab.lib.units import inch\n",
    "from reportlab.lib import colors\n",
    "from reportlab.lib.utils import ImageReader\n",
    "# ---------------- CONFIG ----------------\n",
    "TITLE      = \"Hodge & HodgeClean ‚Äî Equations and Figures\"\n",
    "AUTHOR     = \"David Manning\"\n",
    "AFFIL      = \"Independent Researcher\"\n",
    "EMAIL      = \"david.manning@example.com\"\n",
    "OUT_PDF    = Path(\"HodgeClean_All_Equations_and_Figures.pdf\")\n",
    "SEARCH_ROOTS = [Path(\".\"), Path(\"./reports\"), Path(\"./figures\"), Path(\"./images\")]\n",
    "FIG_EXTS     = {\".png\", \".jpg\", \".jpeg\"}     # PDFs excluded\n",
    "TEX_GLOBS    = [\"**/*.tex\", \"HodgeClean_Framework_Paper*.tex\", \"Verification_Report.tex\"]\n",
    "MAX_W_INCH   = 7.0\n",
    "EQR_DIR      = Path(\".eq_renders\")\n",
    "# -------------- HELPERS ---------------\n",
    "def read_text_safe(p: Path) -> str:\n",
    "    try:    return p.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\", errors=\"ignore\")\n",
    "    except: return \"\"\n",
    "def find_files(roots, exts=None, globs=None):\n",
    "    seen=set()\n",
    "    if globs:\n",
    "        for root in roots:\n",
    "            for g in globs:\n",
    "                for p in root.glob(g):\n",
    "                    if p.is_file():\n",
    "                        rp=p.resolve()\n",
    "                        if rp not in seen:\n",
    "                            seen.add(rp); yield p\n",
    "    if exts:\n",
    "        exts={e.lower() for e in exts}\n",
    "        for root in roots:\n",
    "            for p in root.rglob(\"*\"):\n",
    "                if p.is_file() and p.suffix.lower() in exts:\n",
    "                    rp=p.resolve()\n",
    "                    if rp not in seen:\n",
    "                        seen.add(rp); yield p\n",
    "DISPLAY_PATTERNS = [\n",
    "    (r\"\\\\\\[(?P<body>.+?)\\\\\\]\", re.DOTALL),\n",
    "    (r\"\\$\\$(?P<body>.+?)\\$\\$\", re.DOTALL),\n",
    "    (r\"\\\\begin\\{equation\\*?\\}(?P<body>.+?)\\\\end\\{equation\\*?\\}\", re.DOTALL),\n",
    "    (r\"\\\\begin\\{align\\*?\\}(?P<body>.+?)\\\\end\\{align\\*?\\}\", re.DOTALL),\n",
    "    (r\"\\\\\\((?P<body>.+?)\\\\\\)\", re.DOTALL),\n",
    "    (r\"\\$(?P<body>[^$]+?)\\$\", 0),\n",
    "]\n",
    "LABEL_LIKE = re.compile(r\"\\\\(label|tag|nonumber|notag)\\{.*?\\}\")\n",
    "COMMENT    = re.compile(r\"(?m)%.*?$\")\n",
    "PLACEHOLDER = {r\"\\textit{not recorded}\", \"not recorded\"}\n",
    "def clean_math_body(s:str)->str:\n",
    "    s=COMMENT.sub(\"\", s)\n",
    "    s=LABEL_LIKE.sub(\"\", s)\n",
    "    s=s.strip()\n",
    "    s=re.sub(r\"\\s{2,}\", \" \", s)\n",
    "    return s\n",
    "def looks_like_real_math(s:str)->bool:\n",
    "    if not s: return False\n",
    "    low=s.lower().replace(\" \",\"\")\n",
    "    if any(ph.replace(\" \",\"\") in low for ph in PLACEHOLDER): return False\n",
    "    core=re.sub(r\"[{}\\s\\\\]\",\"\",s)\n",
    "    return len(core)>=3\n",
    "def extract_display_equations(tex:str):\n",
    "    eqs=[]\n",
    "    for pat,fl in DISPLAY_PATTERNS:\n",
    "        for m in re.finditer(pat, tex, fl):\n",
    "            body=clean_math_body(m.group(\"body\"))\n",
    "            if not body: continue\n",
    "            if \"align\" in pat and r\"\\\\\" in body:\n",
    "                for b in [clean_math_body(x) for x in re.split(r\"(?<!\\\\)\\\\\\\\\", body)]:\n",
    "                    if looks_like_real_math(b): eqs.append(b)\n",
    "            else:\n",
    "                if looks_like_real_math(body): eqs.append(body)\n",
    "    seen=set(); out=[]\n",
    "    for e in eqs:\n",
    "        if e not in seen:\n",
    "            seen.add(e); out.append(e)\n",
    "    return out\n",
    "def render_equation_to_png(latex_body:str, out_dir:Path, idx:int)->Path:\n",
    "    out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n",
    "    out_png = out_dir / f\"eq_{idx:04d}.png\"\n",
    "    fig = plt.figure(figsize=(6, 0.01))\n",
    "    ax = fig.add_axes([0,0,1,1]); ax.axis(\"off\")\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        ax.text(0.5, 0.5, f\"${latex_body}$\", ha=\"center\", va=\"center\", fontsize=14)\n",
    "        fig.tight_layout(pad=0.2)\n",
    "        fig.savefig(out_png, dpi=200, transparent=True)\n",
    "    except Exception:\n",
    "        ax.clear(); ax.axis(\"off\")\n",
    "        ax.text(0.0, 1.0, latex_body, ha=\"left\", va=\"top\", fontsize=8, family=\"monospace\")\n",
    "        fig.savefig(out_png, dpi=200, transparent=True)\n",
    "    finally:\n",
    "        plt.close(fig)\n",
    "    return out_png\n",
    "def as_rl_image(img_path:Path, max_w_inch=MAX_W_INCH):\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        im=ImageReader(str(img_path))\n",
    "        iw,ih=im.getSize()\n",
    "        max_w_pt=float(max_w_inch)*float(inch)\n",
    "        scale=min(1.0, max_w_pt/float(iw)) if iw else 1.0\n",
    "        return Image(str(img_path), width=iw*scale, height=ih*scale)\n",
    "    except Exception:\n",
    "        return Paragraph(f\"[unreadable image: {img_path.name}]\", getSampleStyleSheet()[\"Italic\"])\n",
    "# -------------- COLLECT ----------------\n",
    "tex_files = sorted(find_files(SEARCH_ROOTS, globs=TEX_GLOBS), key=lambda p:p.as_posix())\n",
    "fig_files = sorted(find_files(SEARCH_ROOTS, exts=FIG_EXTS),   key=lambda p:p.as_posix())\n",
    "equations=[]\n",
    "for tf in tex_files:\n",
    "    txt=read_text_safe(tf)\n",
    "    for e in extract_display_equations(txt):\n",
    "        equations.append((tf,e))\n",
    "print(f\"Found {len(equations)} filtered equations and {len(fig_files)} raster figures.\")\n",
    "# -------------- STYLES/DOC --------------\n",
    "styles = getSampleStyleSheet()\n",
    "if \"SmallX\" not in styles:\n",
    "    styles.add(ParagraphStyle(name=\"SmallX\", parent=styles[\"BodyText\"], fontSize=9))\n",
    "if \"CaptionX\" not in styles:\n",
    "    styles.add(ParagraphStyle(name=\"CaptionX\", parent=styles[\"BodyText\"], fontSize=9))\n",
    "if \"GreyCaptionX\" not in styles:\n",
    "    styles.add(ParagraphStyle(name=\"GreyCaptionX\", parent=styles[\"BodyText\"],\n",
    "                              fontSize=9, textColor=colors.HexColor(\"#666666\")))\n",
    "doc = SimpleDocTemplate(\n",
    "    str(OUT_PDF),\n",
    "    pagesize=letter,\n",
    "    leftMargin=0.75*inch, rightMargin=0.75*inch,\n",
    "    topMargin=0.75*inch,  bottomMargin=0.75*inch\n",
    ")\n",
    "story=[]\n",
    "# --- Title ---\n",
    "story.append(Paragraph(f\"<para align='center'><b>{TITLE}</b></para>\", styles[\"Title\"]))\n",
    "story.append(Spacer(1, 0.2*inch))\n",
    "meta = f\"{AUTHOR} | {AFFIL} | {EMAIL}\"\n",
    "story.append(Paragraph(f\"<para align='center'>{meta}</para>\", styles[\"Normal\"]))\n",
    "ts = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S UTC\")\n",
    "story.append(Paragraph(f\"<para align='center'>{ts}</para>\", styles[\"SmallX\"]))\n",
    "story.append(PageBreak())\n",
    "# --- Equations ---\n",
    "story.append(Paragraph(\"<b>Equations</b>\", styles[\"Heading2\"]))\n",
    "if not equations:\n",
    "    story.append(Paragraph(\"No equations were discovered in the TeX sources.\", styles[\"SmallX\"]))\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    for i,(src,body) in enumerate(equations,1):\n",
    "        png = render_equation_to_png(body, EQR_DIR, i)\n",
    "        story.append(KeepTogether([\n",
    "            as_rl_image(png),\n",
    "            Spacer(1, 0.05*inch),\n",
    "            Paragraph(f\"Eq. {i:03d} ‚Äî source: {src.name}\", styles[\"GreyCaptionX\"])\n",
    "        ]))\n",
    "        story.append(Spacer(1, 0.15*inch))\n",
    "story.append(PageBreak())\n",
    "# --- Figures (raster only) ---\n",
    "story.append(Paragraph(\"<b>Figures</b>\", styles[\"Heading2\"]))\n",
    "if not fig_files:\n",
    "    story.append(Paragraph(\"No raster figures (.png/.jpg) found.\", styles[\"SmallX\"]))\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    for j,fp in enumerate(fig_files,1):\n",
    "        story.append(KeepTogether([\n",
    "            as_rl_image(fp),\n",
    "            Spacer(1, 0.05*inch),\n",
    "            Paragraph(f\"Figure {j:03d}: {fp.as_posix()}\", styles[\"GreyCaptionX\"])\n",
    "        ]))\n",
    "        story.append(Spacer(1, 0.15*inch))\n",
    "# --- Summary ---\n",
    "story.append(PageBreak())\n",
    "story.append(Paragraph(\"<b>Summary</b>\", styles[\"Heading2\"]))\n",
    "story.append(Paragraph(f\"TeX files scanned: {len(tex_files)}\", styles[\"Normal\"]))\n",
    "story.append(Paragraph(f\"Equations rendered: {len(equations)}\", styles[\"Normal\"]))\n",
    "story.append(Paragraph(f\"Figures found (raster): {len(fig_files)}\", styles[\"Normal\"]))\n",
    "story.append(Paragraph(f\"Generated: {ts}\", styles[\"SmallX\"]))\n",
    "# --- Build ---\n",
    "doc.build(story)\n",
    "print(f\"‚úÖ Built PDF: {OUT_PDF.resolve()}\")\n",
    "size_kb = float(OUT_PDF.stat().st_size) / 1024.0\n",
    "print(f\"   Size: {size_kb:.1f} KB\")"
   ]

    "# === Final Clean + Seal (dedupe + SHA256 + seal confirmation) ===\n",
    "from pathlib import Path\n",
    "import zipfile, tempfile, shutil, hashlib, datetime\n",
    "def seal_final_zip(prefix=\"HodgeClean_Final_Package_\"):\n",
    "    # Locate the newest final package\n",
    "    zips = sorted(Path(\".\").glob(f\"{prefix}*.zip\"))\n",
    "    if not zips:\n",
    "        raise FileNotFoundError(f\"No ZIP found with prefix {prefix}\")\n",
    "    latest = zips[-1]\n",
    "    print(f\"üì¶ Located latest archive ‚Üí {latest.name}\")\n",
    "    # Create a temporary cleaned archive\n",
    "    tmp = tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix=\".zip\")\n",
    "    added = set()\n",
    "    with zipfile.ZipFile(latest, \"r\") as zin, \\\n",
    "         zipfile.ZipFile(tmp.name, \"w\", compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zout:\n",
    "        for item in zin.infolist():\n",
    "            if item.filename not in added:\n",
    "                zout.writestr(item, zin.read(item.filename))\n",
    "                added.add(item.filename)\n",
    "            else:\n",
    "                print(f\"‚ö†Ô∏è  Removed duplicate: {item.filename}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"üßπ Clean rewrite complete ‚Äî {len(added)} unique files retained.\")\n",
    "    # Replace old archive with the cleaned one\n",
    "    shutil.move(tmp.name, latest)\n",
    "    # Compute SHA256\n",
    "    sha = hashlib.sha256(Path(latest).read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n",
    "    ts = datetime.datetime.now(datetime.timezone.utc).strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S UTC\")\n",
    "    # Rename sealed version\n",
    "    sealed = latest.with_name(latest.stem + \"_SEALED\" + latest.suffix)\n",
    "    latest.rename(sealed)\n",
    "    print(f\"üîí Renamed archive ‚Üí {sealed.name}\")\n",
    "    # Write seal metadata\n",
    "    meta = Path(\"HodgeClean_FinalSeal_Metadata.txt\")\n",
    "    meta.write_text(\n",
    "        f\"HodgeClean Framework ‚Äì Canonical Sealed Archive\\n\"\n",
    "        f\"Timestamp : {ts}\\n\"\n",
    "        f\"Archive   : {sealed.name}\\n\"\n",
    "        f\"SHA-256   : {sha}\\n\"\n",
    "        f\"Files     : {len(added)}\\n\"\n",
    "        f\"Status    : Immutable canonical version\\n\"\n",
    "    )\n",
    "    print(f\"üßæ Metadata written ‚Üí {meta.resolve()}\")\n",
    "    print(\"\\nŒ© SEAL COMPLETE ‚Äì canonical archive ready for publication ‚úÖ\")\n",
    "    print(f\"SHA-256 : {sha}\")\n",
    "# Run the seal\n",
    "seal_final_zip()"
   ]

    "from pathlib import Path\n",
    "from datetime import datetime, timezone\n",

    "# Locate the sealed ZIP\n",
    "zips = sorted(Path(\".\").glob(\"HodgeClean_Final_Package_*_SEALED.zip\"))\n",

   "source": [
    "# === OA original export: artifact index (archive view) ===\n",
    "from pathlib import Path\n",
    "import json\n",
    "\n",
    "root = Path(\".\")\n",
    "\n",
    "png_files: list[str] = []\n",
    "csv_files: list[str] = []\n",
    "json_files: list[str] = []\n",
    "log_files: list[str] = []\n",
    "ipynb_files: list[str] = []\n",
    "zip_files: list[str] = []\n",
    "other_files: list[str] = []\n",
    "\n",
    "for p in root.rglob(\"*\"):\n",
    "    if not p.is_file():\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "    rel = str(p.relative_to(root))\n",
    "    suf = p.suffix.lower()\n",
    "    if suf == \".png\":\n",
    "        png_files.append(rel)\n",
    "    elif suf == \".csv\":\n",
    "        csv_files.append(rel)\n",
    "    elif suf == \".json\":\n",
    "        json_files.append(rel)\n",
    "    elif suf == \".log\":\n",
    "        log_files.append(rel)\n",
    "    elif suf == \".ipynb\":\n",
    "        ipynb_files.append(rel)\n",
    "    elif suf in {\".zip\", \".tar\", \".gz\"}:\n",
    "        zip_files.append(rel)\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        other_files.append(rel)\n",
    "\n",
    "def print_section(title: str, files: list[str]) -> None:\n",
    "    print(f\"\\nüìÇ {title}: {len(files)} file(s)\")\n",
    "    for f in sorted(files):\n",
    "        print(f\"   ‚îî {f}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"Running archive artifact index...\\n\")\n",
    "\n",
    "print_section(\"plots (PNG)\", png_files)\n",
    "print_section(\"data tables (CSV)\", csv_files)\n",
    "print_section(\"JSON summaries / settings\", json_files)\n",
    "print_section(\"log files\", log_files)\n",
    "print_section(\"notebooks (ipynb)\", ipynb_files)\n",
    "print_section(\"archives (ZIP/TAR/etc.)\", zip_files)\n",
    "print_section(\"other files\", other_files)\n",
    "\n",
    "total_files = (\n",
    "    len(png_files)\n",
    "    + len(csv_files)\n",
    "    + len(json_files)\n",
    "    + len(log_files)\n",
    "    + len(ipynb_files)\n",
    "    + len(zip_files)\n",
    "    + len(other_files)\n",
    ")\n",
    "\n",
    "manifest = {\n",
    "    \"category\": \"original_OA_export_archive\",\n",
    "    \"total_files\": int(total_files),\n",
    "    \"sections\": {\n",
    "        \"plots_png\": sorted(png_files),\n",
    "        \"data_csv\": sorted(csv_files),\n",
    "        \"json\": sorted(json_files),\n",
    "        \"logs\": sorted(log_files),\n",
    "        \"notebooks\": sorted(ipynb_files),\n",
    "        \"archives\": sorted(zip_files),\n",
    "        \"other\": sorted(other_files),\n",
    "    },\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "out_path = root / \"OA_original_export_index.json\"\n",
    "with out_path.open(\"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n",
    "    json.dump(manifest, f, indent=2)\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f\"\\n‚úÖ Archive artifact index complete.\")\n",
    "print(f\"   Total files detected: {total_files}\")\n",
    "print(f\"   Summary written to: {out_path.name}\")"
